    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2091057756" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2091057756" />
    <a title="Sha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7081058-sha"><img alt="Sha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484503062p2/7081058.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2091057756?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sha" href="/user/show/7081058-sha">Sha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2091057756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5106226554621830059"><i> "You know, you're kind of a dramatic person, Elliot," she said mildly. <br/><br/>"I am not! How dare you!"<br/><br/>"It's not a bad thing," Myra said, "but when a boy calls a girl the nightlight of his soul, other people might be forgiven for thinking he's being intentionally over the top."</i><br/><br/>Elliot Schafer, irritable resident of Earth, finds himself in a quasi-Medieval magic school. People are talking about warrior-training (UGH, says Elliot) and all of it looks a lot like child endangerment. BUT, there are elves. S</span>
  <span id="freeText5106226554621830059" style="display:none"><i> "You know, you're kind of a dramatic person, Elliot," she said mildly. <br /><br />"I am not! How dare you!"<br /><br />"It's not a bad thing," Myra said, "but when a boy calls a girl the nightlight of his soul, other people might be forgiven for thinking he's being intentionally over the top."</i><br /><br />Elliot Schafer, irritable resident of Earth, finds himself in a quasi-Medieval magic school. People are talking about warrior-training (UGH, says Elliot) and all of it looks a lot like child endangerment. BUT, there are elves. Specifically, there is Serene-Heart-in-the-Chaos-of-Battle, the Border Guard's first elven recruit, and Elliot falls in love at first sight. So he decides to stay despite the presence of musclehead types like that really annoying Luke Sunborn person. <br /><br />Let me be clear. This is not an epic journey through the otherlands or a massive worldbuilding adventure with quests goals. This is a very personal, very emotional journey of HOW DO YOU DO RELATIONSHIPS starring Elliot Schafer, who is to conversations what machine guns are to knife-fights. Every other word out of his mouth is an insult and I am continuously amazed that people don't try to strangle him more than they actually do. Elliot is... SPIKY. He is so spiky. He is a hedgehog in human form. I love him so much that I sometimes stare at the ceiling and have feelings about Elliot trying to make sense of relationships. It's very teenage, and I usually hate that, but there's so much WANT and NEED and NEVERTHELESS YOU ARE MY FRIENDS that I am touched rather than annoyed. <br /><br />The other two spokes of the trio are just as dear to me. Luke is a sweetheart of a Disney Princess who is nevertheless bound by the thought processes of his world and his life, and Serene is the most hilarious method of calling out the patriarchy that I have ever encountered. Her sincere confusion about all the sensitive human men killing people in the face and not doing manly things like embroidery never ceases to be a delight, and I'm continuously thrilled by the fact that Serene is the elven version of the too-cool-for-you Bad Boy with a Heart of Gold. Gender roles get lined up and shot at a lot, and I'm always a fan of that.<br /><br />This collected and remastered version of the original <i>The Turn of the Story</i> features a few extra filler scenes, as well as Elliot-PoV version of <i>Wings in the Morning</i>, so you have new reading material even if you have the entirety of <i>The Turn of the Story</i> saved into your laptop like I do.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5106226554621830059" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2344515962" />
    <a title="Hollis " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16668577-hollis"><img alt="Hollis " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586714618p2/16668577.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2344515962?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hollis " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hollis " href="/user/show/16668577-hollis">Hollis </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=all-the-lols">all-the-lols</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=genre-bending">genre-bending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=lgbtqia">lgbtqia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=heroes-to-root-for">heroes-to-root-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=library-read">library-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=hello-diversity">hello-diversity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=seriously-kick-ass-lady-protag">seriously-kick-ass-lady-protag</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2344515962" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17768010675700802396"><i>Even if you found yourself in a magical story, there were no guarantees that you were the hero, or that you would get the things you dreamed of. Elliot knew no way, being who he was, to deserve that.</i><br/><br/>IN OTHER LANDS is subversive, silly, sassy, strange, and sweet. It's also a wee bit heartbreaking. And sometimes you kinda wonder if anything is happening, and what's even going on, and maybe Elliot is like super abrasive and awful (kinda like how Hermione could've been if she was completely without </span>
  <span id="freeText17768010675700802396" style="display:none"><i>Even if you found yourself in a magical story, there were no guarantees that you were the hero, or that you would get the things you dreamed of. Elliot knew no way, being who he was, to deserve that.</i><br /><br />IN OTHER LANDS is subversive, silly, sassy, strange, and sweet. It's also a wee bit heartbreaking. And sometimes you kinda wonder if anything is happening, and what's even going on, and maybe Elliot is like super abrasive and awful (kinda like how Hermione could've been if she was completely without filter and did not absorb her besties' social skills), but then you're charmed by the whole thing all over again, marvel at all the gender reversal and discussion over traditional roles turned on their heads, and get to experience a fantasy story where the lead character avoids all sorts of violent conflict, preferring to use words and treaties instead of fists and war. <br /><br />"<i>I don't need you to explain to me the concept of a magical land filled with fantastic creatures that only certain special children can enter. I am acquainted with the last several centuries of popular culture. There are books. And cartoons, for the illiterate.</i>"<br /><br />This book is a whole lot of things. <br /><br />"<i>All right then. Tell me about computers.</i>"<br />"<b>Well.. they're boxes.. but you can write things in them. And read things in them. And there are cats in them who are funny for some reason. They're like -- boxes of infinity. And! You keep the wikipedia in them!</b>"<br />"<i>[..] Hold that thought, because it might be my favourite thing you have ever said. It might be my favourite thing anybody has ever said.</i>"<br /><br />Also I just really wanted to include that exchange about computers because it was the best. Seriously, this book might've been really long, and sometimes I wish it had been less so, but it also made me laugh a lot and it was also really smart. But I can totally see how this won't be the kind of thing that'll work for everyone.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17768010675700802396" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2109895512" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2109895512" />
    <a title="- ̗̀ DANY  ̖́- (danyreads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47960008---dany---danyreads"><img alt="- ̗̀ DANY  ̖́- (danyreads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477097603p2/47960008.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2109895512?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="- ̗̀ DANY  ̖́- (danyreads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="- ̗̀ DANY  ̖́- (danyreads)" href="/user/show/47960008---dany---danyreads">- ̗̀ DANY  ̖́- (danyreads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47960008---dany---danyreads?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47960008---dany---danyreads?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47960008---dany---danyreads?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2109895512" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6156683310174310235"><b>. : ☾⋆ — 5 ★ </b><br/><br/>READ THIS REVIEW ON MY BLOG!!!<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://bit.ly/2AXEB49'>https://bit.ly/2AXEB49</a><br/><br/>oh my, this is it. <br/>this is the cutest, warmest, coziest, most wholesome, nourishing, organic, pleasant, sincere, wholeheartedly pure, most adorable book in the entire world. <br/><br/>In Other Lands is not a perfect book, though, and I’ll give you that. but it’s a book that pulls sharply at your heartstrings and strikes a chord deep in your tummy and just gives you this all-encompassing feeling of absolute and excellent warmth and pleasantne</span>
  <span id="freeText6156683310174310235" style="display:none"><b>. : ☾⋆ — 5 ★ </b><br /><br />READ THIS REVIEW ON MY BLOG!!!<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bit.ly/2AXEB49">https://bit.ly/2AXEB49</a><br /><br />oh my, this is it. <br />this is the cutest, warmest, coziest, most wholesome, nourishing, organic, pleasant, sincere, wholeheartedly pure, most adorable book in the entire world. <br /><br />In Other Lands is not a perfect book, though, and I’ll give you that. but it’s a book that pulls sharply at your heartstrings and strikes a chord deep in your tummy and just gives you this all-encompassing feeling of absolute and excellent warmth and pleasantness and just... I’m running out of adjectives here. I’m not even remotely exaggerating, though. In Other Lands was a delight, and I’m so mad I ever hesitated to pick it up just because I felt intimidated by its 437-page length. I truly am and will forever be terrified of big books but this is not by any means a tedious or tiring read. I think that’s quite an impressive feat also, considering the fact that this book narrates these characters’ lives from age 13 to age 17, exploring everything from sexuality, family, personal growth, etc. four years is a REALLY long time within a book’s timespan and achieving it in a way that doesn’t feel rushed or monotonous, and instead finds a perfect balance between character development and fun little bits of action is totally an accomplishment and I ADORE Sarah Rees Brennan for it. she’s so talented and she did an incredible job!!! <br /><br />I’m still feeling a little overwhelmed by this book so I really don’t think there’s much else to say other than I loved this with every piece of my heart. the characters, the plot, the setting, the humor, everything was beyond what I ever could’ve expected and I’m absolutely smitten. it’s a book that stays with you forever, and (right now) it is, and will probably continue to be, one of the very best books I’ve ever had the pleasure of reading. I can’t recommend it enough. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6156683310174310235" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('o0ZCaVmkeEANGQ5DuB+K/hApDS7tXVH2BAVWytVchE07gjABByMtZF1F0mUr74Jll0HhCPokDTqrKhq63FjFGw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TEcgjOrE95aQnQfHRyWlg64IrwLcZSaPX5vj0Z0KtQnUg1LktEOissDB2+HU1a0YKWBDJMscekPwtK+hlA70Xw==')})
  }
